      <p>[yoonkook au] where twitter exists in ancient greece, jungkook is hercules, and yoongi is an annoyed citizen who just wants to go about his day without hearing how great this new demigod is</p><p> <img src="https://taehyikes.github.io/socmed/hercules/001%E2%80%941.jpg" align = "center" width = "90%" /> </p><p> <img src="https://taehyikes.github.io/socmed/hercules/001%E2%80%942.jpg" align = "center" width = "90%" /> </p><p> <img src="https://taehyikes.github.io/socmed/hercules/001%E2%80%943.jpg" align = "center" width = "90%" /> </p><p> <img src="https://taehyikes.github.io/socmed/hercules/001%E2%80%944.jpg" align = "center" width = "90%" /> </p><p>based on this brain spiral</p><p>notes:
‚Ä¢kinda modern times kinda ancient greece, idk it‚Äôs gonna be silly, and pls, it‚Äôs ALL PRETEND
‚Ä¢gonna post this over maybe 2 weeks?
‚Ä¢my fellow history buffs, if ur looking for accuracy of myths, look away now, i‚Äôm making twt exist in ancient greece, there r no facts here</p><p>profiles 1/3: 
‚Ä¢jungkook is hercules and genuinely just here to save some folks, the sweetest and strongest bean in all of greece
‚Ä¢seokjin is jungkook‚Äôs trainer, and has basically raised him from gawky awkward teen to strong awkward hero</p><p> <img src="https://taehyikes.github.io/socmed/hercules/004%E2%80%941.jpg" align = "center" width = "90%" /> </p><p> <img src="https://taehyikes.github.io/socmed/hercules/004%E2%80%942.jpg" align = "center" width = "90%" /> </p><p>profiles 2/3:
